=== ECOLOGICAL RELEVANCE ===
Vegetation and forest cover data indicates tree species composition. Chanterelles form mycorrhizal associations primarily with conifers — especially Douglas-fir, Sitka spruce, western hemlock, and western red cedar, all common in the Ucluelet region.
